- **Today**: 248 consecutive days with ZERO father-child contact

### Constitutional Significance

- *Troxel v Granville*, 530 US 57 (2000): Fundamental parental right
- *Pierron v Pierron*, 486 Mich 81 (2010): Due process in custody
- MCL 722.27a: Parenting time presumed in child's best interest
